# Stealth Machine — Full Benchmark Summary

**Machine:** stealth (AMD) — Ryzen 7 3700X, RTX 2080 SUPER 8GB VRAM, 32GB RAM  
**Tool:** llama-benchy 0.3.5 | **Date:** 2026-04-10  
**Method:** 3 runs per test, latency mode: generation, GPU/CPU temps polled every 2s

---

## Cross-Model Comparison

### Generation Throughput (TG tok/s)

| Model | Size | tg=64 @ pp=512 | tg=256 @ pp=512 | tg=64 @ pp=2048 | tg=256 @ pp=2048 | Tested from | Date |
|:------|-----:|---:|---:|---:|---:|:------|:------|
| gemma3:4b | 3.2GB | 102.2 | 101.0 | ~102 | ~101 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |
| nemotron-mini | 2.6GB | 81.4 | 91.8 | ~81 | ~92 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |
| qwen2.5-coder:7b | 4.5GB | 77.8 | 77.4 | ~78 | ~77 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |
| llama3.1:8b | 4.7GB | 74.8 | 74.3 | ~75 | ~74 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |
| qwen3:8b | 4.9GB | 73.6 | 73.1 | ~74 | ~73 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |
| deepseek-r1:8b | 4.9GB | 73.3 | 72.9 | ~73 | ~73 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |
| gemma4:e2b | 6.8GB | 43.3 | 43.2 | 43.9 | 42.2 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-18 |
| gemma4:26b ⚠️ | 17.2GB | 15.1 | 14.8 | 13.6 | 13.5 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-18 |
| qwen3:14b | 8.7GB | 12.5 | 12.4 | 11.6 | 11.6 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |
| qwen2.5-coder:14b | 8.4GB | 10.7 | 10.7 | ~11 | ~11 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |
| deepseek-r1:14b | 8.4GB | 10.8 | 10.6 | 10.8 | 10.6 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |
| phi4 (14B) | 8.5GB | 10.7 | 10.7 | 10.7 | 10.7 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |
| qwen3.6 ⚠️ | 22.8GB | 6.81 | 7.05 | 6.60 | 6.96 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-18 |
| qwen3:32b ⚠️ | 19.3GB | 3.0 | 3.0 | 3.0 | 3.0 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |

> ⚠️ gemma4:26b has ~9GB RAM spill (17.2GB model, 8GB VRAM). MoE architecture keeps TG faster than dense 14B models despite spill, but TTFT is ~3× worse.  
> ⚠️ qwen3:32b has ~11GB RAM spill — bottlenecked by system memory bandwidth, not VRAM.  
> ⚠️ qwen3.6 has ~14.8GB RAM spill (22.8GB model, 8GB VRAM) — heavily memory-bandwidth-bound; slower TG than smaller models.

| qwen3:8b | ~1,891 | 357 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |

| phi4 (14B) | ~844 | 746 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |
| qwen3:14b | ~710 | 898 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |
| deepseek-r1:14b | ~608 | 966 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |
| qwen3.6 ⚠️ | ~374 | 1,905 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-18 |
| qwen3:32b | ~200 | 3,153 | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 |

### Thermal Profile (peak across all tests)

| Model | GPU peak | CPU peak | Tested from | Date | Notes |
|:------|---:|---:|:------|:------|:------|
| gemma4:e2b | 48°C | 67°C | stealth (local) | 2026-04-18 | Coolest GPU — low util (~25-52%) despite near-full VRAM |
| nemotron-mini | 54°C | 54°C | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 | Lightest overall thermal load |
| qwen2.5-coder:7b | 58°C | 57°C | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 | |
| gemma3:4b | 61°C | 59°C | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 | |
| llama3.1:8b | 64°C | 59°C | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 | |
| qwen3:8b | 68°C | 60°C | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 | |
| deepseek-r1:8b | 68°C | 62°C | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 | |
| qwen2.5-coder:14b | 59°C | 71°C | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 | CPU higher — VRAM pressure |
| phi4 (14B) | 61°C | 71°C | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 | |
| qwen3:14b | 60°C | 70°C | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 | |
| deepseek-r1:14b | 57°C | 70°C | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 | |
| gemma4:26b ⚠️ | 54°C | 73°C | stealth (local) | 2026-04-18 | ~9GB RAM spill; GPU spiky (0→93% bursts) |
| qwen3.6 ⚠️ | 54°C | 72°C | stealth (local) | 2026-04-18 | ~14.8GB RAM spill (22.8GB model); GPU bursts to 90% during prefill only |
| qwen3:32b | 60°C | **79°C** | stealth (local) | 2026-04-10 | CPU elevated by RAM spill |

---

## Swarm Routing Recommendations

| Route | Current model | Verdict | Alternative |
|:------|:-------------|:--------|:------------|
| conversational (M4) | qwen3:8b | ✅ Stays on M4 | — |
| general/research | qwen3:14b | ✅ Best 14B reasoning | — |
| code | qwen2.5-coder:14b | ✅ Solid, matches qwen3:14b TG speed | qwen2.5-coder:7b for 6× faster TG |
| verify (2-pass CoT) | deepseek-r1:14b | ⚠️ Slowest 14B PP (608 tok/s) | deepseek-r1:8b = 73 tok/s TG, much faster |
| heavy verify | qwen3:32b | ⚠️ 3 tok/s TG — use sparingly | phi4 as faster 14B alternative |

---

## Key Takeaways

- **8B models are 6× faster** than 14B on this GPU (73 vs 12 tok/s TG) — worth routing shorter tasks to 8B
- **nemotron-mini is the fastest** for PP throughput (4,318 tok/s) and coolest thermals — ideal for high-volume tasks
- **deepseek-r1:8b matches llama3.1:8b and qwen3:8b** in TG speed (~73 tok/s) but brings native CoT — strong candidate for verify route
- **qwen3:32b is throttled by RAM spill** (3 tok/s) — only use for tasks where quality justifies the wait
- **CPU is the bottleneck for 32b**, not GPU — Ryzen 7 3700X memory bandwidth limits RAM-spill models
- **gemma4:e2b fills the gap between 8B and 14B** — 43 tok/s TG and blazing PP (~3,400 tok/s @ pp=512), but slower than 8B models on TG; mostly running from RAM (only ~1.9GB VRAM active)
- **gemma4:26b MoE beats 14B dense models in TG** (15 vs 12 tok/s) despite being 17GB — MoE only activates 4B params per token so compute is light; TTFT penalty is severe (1,430ms) due to ~9GB RAM spill; not worth routing to unless quality demands it
- **qwen3.6 (22.8GB) is the most RAM-spill-bound model tested** — ~14.8GB spills to system RAM; 7 tok/s TG and ~374 tok/s PP @ pp=512; TTFT ~1,900ms; only practical for tasks where quality justifies significant latency

---

*Full per-model reports with temperature charts follow below.*

# Benchmark Report: qwen3:14b

**Date:** 2026-04-10 15:46  
**Target machine:** stealth — RTX 2080 SUPER 8GB VRAM, Ryzen 7 3700X, 32GB RAM  
**Endpoint:** http://100.118.160.122:11434/v1  
**Tested from:** stealth (AMD) — local  
**Runs per test:** 3

### Temperatures & Utilization

```mermaid
xychart-beta
```
```mermaid
  title "Temperature — pp=2048 tg=64"
```

---

## Finance Model Benchmarks — 2026-04-11

**Target machine:** stealth — RTX 2080 SUPER 8GB VRAM, Ryzen 7 3700X, 32GB RAM
**Settings:** Q8 KV cache + Flash Attention enabled (new as of this session)
**Runs per test:** 3 | PP sizes: 128, 512, 2048 | TG sizes: 64, 256

### TG Decode Speed (tok/s)

| Model | Base | tg64 pp128 | tg256 pp128 | tg64 pp2048 | tg256 pp2048 | GPU peak |
|-------|------|-----------|------------|------------|-------------|----------|
| 0xroyce/plutus | Llama 3.1 8B | 67.7 | 67.3 | 64.4 | 64.6 | 58°C |
| brrndnn/mistral7b-finance | Mistral 7B | 66.4 | 65.8 | 62.4 | 62.2 | 66°C |
| jjansen/adapt-finance-llama2-7b | Llama 2 7B | 92.0 | 92.3 | 83.7 | 83.3 | 64°C |

### PP Prefill Speed (tok/s)

| Model | pp128 | pp512 | pp2048 |
|-------|-------|-------|--------|
| 0xroyce/plutus | 3598 | 2270 | 2069 |
| brrndnn/mistral7b-finance | 1709–1823 | 1696–1760 | 1632–1633 |
| jjansen/adapt-finance-llama2-7b | 272* | 2394–2974 | 2595–2604 |

*adapt-finance pp128 anomaly — likely model loading during first test; pp512+ numbers are valid.

### TTFT

| Model | pp128 | pp512 | pp2048 |
|-------|-------|-------|--------|
| 0xroyce/plutus | ~195ms | ~362ms | ~1050ms |
| brrndnn/mistral7b-finance | ~106ms | ~331ms | ~1274ms |
| jjansen/adapt-finance-llama2-7b | ~43ms | ~193ms | ~839ms |

### Notes

- **adapt-finance-llama2-7b is the fastest decoder** at ~83–92 tok/s — significantly faster than both other finance models and most general models tested. Llama 2 7B architecture runs very efficiently on the 2080 Super.
- **Plutus** is the most consistent — flat decode speed regardless of context depth, lowest temps.
- **mistral7b-finance** is the slowest PP and runs hottest — least efficient of the three.
- **M4:** adapt-finance-llama2-7b also installed locally (no benchmark — no nvidia-smi on Apple Silicon).
- Full per-test reports with temp charts: `~/bench-results/` on stealth.

# Benchmark Report: gemma4:26b

**Date:** 2026-04-18 17:08  
**Target machine:** stealth — RTX 2080 SUPER 8GB VRAM, Ryzen 7 3700X, 32GB RAM

**Runs per test:** 3  
**Notes:** 17.2GB model, ~9GB RAM spill. `--no-cache` flag used. GPU util is bursty (0% during RAM→VRAM loading, 65-93% during compute bursts). MoE: 26B total params, ~4B active per token.
